APPENDIX A.


List of copper-plates examined during the year 1928-29.

Placement
The Collector of Ganjam
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
…
Language
Sanskṛit in Telugu
Origin
Returned
Remarks
Incomplete. In characters of about the 6th century A.D. Relates to the foundation of an agrahāra called Niṅgoṇḍi-agrahāra in Astihōṇarāma-grāma.
ARIE/1928-1929/A/1928-29/2 (page 4)
Placement
Mr. B.R.Vyasarayachar, B.A., B.L., Advocate, Mangalore, South Kanara district.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Kali 4488, Śaka 1309, 1033935 days, Prabhava, Pausha, śu. tṛi-tīyã, Friday, Uttarāshāḍhā, Āyushmad-yōga, Bālavā-karaṇa, Sun in Makara.
Language
Sanskṛit in Kannaḍa
Origin
Returned
Remarks
Records grant, after purchase, of lands in several specified villages, by Mādhavārya, governor of Goa, for offerings and worship to the temple of Subrah-maṇya at Kukke, a part of Kaḍaba, in Tuḷu-maṇḍala.
ARIE/1928-1929/A/1928-29/3 (page 4)
Placement
The Subrahmaṇya temple at Kukke, through Mr. K.R. Achar, M.A., B.L., Advocate, Mangalore.
Dynasty
Vijayana-gara.
King
Pratāpa Bukka-Mahārāya, son of Vīra-Harihararāya.
Date
Śaka 1329, Vyaya, Chaitra, śu. 1.
Language
Kannaḍa in Nāgarī
Origin
Returned
Remarks
Records grant of taxes for offerings to the temple at Kukke, while Bāvappa-Voḍeya of Gōve was governing Maṅgaḷūra-rājya under the orders of the king.
ARIE/1928-1929/A/1928-29/4 (page 4)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1603, Dundu-bhi, Mārgaśira, śu. 15.
Language
Kannaḍa
Origin
Returned
Remarks
Registers a grant of land at Kuḍiginahaḷḷi alias Veṅ-kaṭāpura by Veṅkaṭādri-Nāyaka, son of Kṛishṇappa-Nāyaka and grandson of Veṅkaṭappa-Nāyaka of Bēlūr, to a certain Tippaiya, for offerings, etc., to the temple of Subrahmaṇya at Kukke.
ARIE/1928-1929/A/1928-29/5 (page 4)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Vijayana-gara
King
Śrīraṅgarāyadēva-Mahārāya, ‘ruling from Ghanagiri.’
Date
Śaka 1631, (mistake for 1621), Bahu-dhānya, Āśvija, śu. 15.
Language
Kannaḍa
Origin
Returned
Remarks
Registers gift of the village of Subbarāyapura in Māga-ḍi-sīme to the temple of Subrahmaṇya for daily offer-ings, worship and lamps, by Mummaḍi Doḍḍa-Vīrap-pa-Gauḍa, son of Mummaḍi Kempē-Gauḍa and grand-son of Immaḍi Kempē-Gauḍa of the Sadaśiva-gōtra, the lord of Elahaṁka-nāḍu. This gift is said to have been made by the donor in gratitude for the birth of a son to him called Kempē-Vīra-Gauḍa.
ARIE/1928-1929/A/1928-29/6 (page 4)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Mysore
King
Dēvarāja-Mahīpāla, son of Dēvarāja-Voḍeya, ‘ruling from Śrīraṅgapaṭṭaṇa’.
Date
Śaka 1587 (expired), Viśvāvasu, Pushya, śu. 3, Friday, Makara-saṅkrānti.
Language
Kannaḍa
Origin
Returned
Remarks
Gift of 3 villages, one belonging to the Śrīraṅgapaṭṭaṇa division and the other two to Hāsana, by a certain Dhanōjayya, son of Śivuja and grandson of Nānaja of Lambakarṇa-gōtra and the Āśvalāyana-sūtra, for the celebration of the car-festival in the temple of Sub-rahmaṇya and for the maintenance of an anna-satra.
ARIE/1928-1929/A/1928-29/7 (page 4)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1595, Pramādi, Mārgaśira, śu. 15, Saturday.
Language
Kannaḍa
Origin
Returned
Remarks
Records that Śaṅkaradēvī-Ballāḷati of Kollimogaru received 8 Ikkēri-gadyāṇas (12 varāhas) from Gōpā-layya and agreed to burn a perpetual lamp in the temple of Subrahmaṇya at Kukke. She also under-took to supply rice for daily offerings to the deity with the interest on another sum of 8 gadyāṇa endowed by one Krishṇaya, a relation of Gōpãlayya.
ARIE/1928-1929/A/1928-29/8 (page 4)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Vijayana-gara.
King
Śrīraṅgarāyadēva-Mahārāya, ‘ruling from Vēlāpuri (Vēlūr)’.
Date
Śaka 1588, Viśvā-vasu, Chaitra, śu. 1.
Language
Kannaḍa
Origin
Returned
Remarks
Refers to Āravīṭi Raṅgapparājayya and Gōpāla-rājayya of Sōmavaṁśa, the grandfather and father respectively of the king. Records, that on behalf of the king Raghu-Nãyaka, son of Narasanna and grandson of Rāyasam Tirumalayya granted the vil-lage of Kōgaravaḷḷi in Bēlūrasthala for the feeding to be conducted in the temple of Subrahmaṇya.

Kannaḍa

Returned
Remarks
Mentions the father and grandfather of the king, namely, Gōpāla and Āravīṭi Rāmarāju-Raṅgaparāju. Records the grant by the king of the villages--Haḷe-Bēlūru in Maḷali-Hōbaḷi and Doḍasāgara, a part of Bayikēri in Kebbeṭṭu-nāḍu of Bēlūrusthala, and a field in Kōgaḍavaḷḷi in Kebbeṭṭu-nāḍu, for offerings to the temple of Subrahmaṇya and for feeding (pilgrims).
ARIE/1928-1929/A/1928-29/12 (page 5)
Placement
The President, District Temple Committee, Udipi, South Kanara district.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Dēvarāya-Mahārāja
Date
Śaka 1346, Krōdhi, Pushya, śu. sha-shṭhī, Wednes-day, Makara-saṅkrānti.
Language
Sanskṛit & Kannaḍa
Origin
Returned
Remarks
Gives the genealogy of the king. Records that at the request of Vardhamāna-Bhaṭṭāraka of Sarasvatī-gachchha, Balātkāra-gaṇa and Mūla-saṅgha, the king granted the village of Varāṅga as sarvamānya, for worship and offerings to the image of Nēminātha in the village, and for feeding ascetics.

Returned

States that this copper-plate deed registers sale of lands at Brahmāra-Chētāra by Iśvara-Uṅga-rapaḷḷi and his brother's son Nāraṇa, to a certain Mallapa-Seṭṭi, and his brother Sōvappa-Seṭṭi, sons of Lakkhi-Seṭṭi for 150 honnu.
ARIE/1928-1929/A/1928-29/14 (page 5)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Vijayana-gara.
King
Harihara-Mahārāya
Date
Śaka 1312, Vibhava, Bhādrapada, ba. 10, Thursday.
Language
Kannaḍa
Origin
Returned
Remarks
Refers to Mallapa-Voḍeya of Honnāura, as governing Bārakūru by order of Mahāpradhāna Guṇḍapa-Dāṇ-ṇāyaka. Records an endowment of lands by a certain Māyaṁṇa, brother of Dēvarasa of Kōḷūru, for the maintenance of a feeding-choultry attached to the temple of Sōmayadēva. The land was left in charge of five persons.

APPENDIX B.


Stone inscriptions copied in 1928-29.


TINNEVELLY DISTRICT


SRIVAIKUNTAM TALUK


ARIE/1928-1929/Stone inscriptions copied in 1928-29/1928-29/1 (page 6)
Placement
Tirukkalur.--On a slab set up at the bridge near the village.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Kollam 922, Pra-bhava, [Ā]ṉi 11, [Wednesday], Anusham, trayōdaśī.
Language
Tamil
Remarks
States that the [Kūḷai]vāykkāl of Tirukkōḷūr the sluices to it and other irrigation works, were completed in the year.

NANGUNERI TALUK


ARIE/1928-1929/Stone inscriptions copied in 1928-29/1928-29/2 (page 6)
Placement
Dalapatisamudram.--On the north and west walls of the central shrine in the Tirunāgēś-vara temple at the village.
Dynasty
Pāṇḍya
King
Māṟavarman alias Tribhuvanchakravartin Sundara-Pāṇḍyadēva, ‘who was pleased to present the Chōḷa country’.
Date
8th year and 239th day.
Language
Tamil
Remarks
Begins with the introduction pUmaruviya tirumaTantai etc. Records that at the request of the Śivabrāhmaṇas and Sthānapatis of the temple of Tirunāgēśvaram at Perumba-ḻañji in Nāṭṭāṟṟuppōkku and of the queen Ulaga-muḻuduḍaiyāḷ, the king, while seated on the throne called Maḻavarāyaṉ at Madura, exempted from taxes certain lands, to provide for offerings and worship to the images of Kūttāḍundēvar and his consort, set up in the temple by Kaṇṇaṉ-Kōvaṉ alias Vīranārāyaṇadēvaṉ.
ARIE/1928-1929/Stone inscriptions copied in 1928-29/1928-29/3 (page 6)
Placement
On the south wall of the same shrine.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
17th year
Language
Tamil
Remarks
Registers that the king (name not specified), while seated in his palace at Aḷḷiyūr alias Kēraḷakulāśani-chaturvēdi-maṅgalam in Nāṭṭāṟṟuppōkku, exempted from payment of taxes certain lands granted to the temples of Tirunāgīśvaram-Uḍaiyār Varaguṇa-īśvaram-Uḍaiyār and Puravuvari īvaram-Uḍaiyār at Perumbaḻañji.
ARIE/1928-1929/Stone inscriptions copied in 1928-29/1928-29/4 (page 6)
Placement
On the same wall
Dynasty
…

…
Date
…
Language
Tamil

Records an order stating that uḷvari should be given in respect of certain tax-free gifts of land made at Āvūr to provide for worship in the temples mentioned in No. 3 above.
ARIE/1928-1929/Stone inscriptions copied in 1928-29/1928-29/5 (page 6)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
17th year
Language
Tamil
Remarks
Registers the order issued to the officials of the temples mentioned in No. 3 above, stating that the śrīmukha and uḷvari having been issued, the lands granted may be taken possession of.
ARIE/1928-1929/Stone inscriptions copied in 1928-29/1928-29/6 (page 6)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Pāṇḍya
King
Jaṭāvarman alias Tribhuvanachakravartin, Śrīvallabhadēva.
Date
4th year
Language
Tamil
Remarks
Commences with the introduction tirumaTantai, etc. States that on the representation made by Mānābharaṇ-attu-Ayyaṉ, one vēli of land belonging to the three temples mentioned in No. 3 above was exempted from taxes. Mentions the throne Pāṇḍyarājaṉ in the palace at Madurai, on which the king was seated while making the grant. On a pillar in the verandah round the shrine, is engraved a portion of a record dated in the 4th year of an unspecified king.
ARIE/1928-1929/Stone inscriptions copied in 1928-29/1928-29/7 (page 6)
Placement
On the base of the verandah round the same shrine.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Śrīvallabhadēva
Date
…
Language
Tamil
Remarks
States that the king, while seated on his throne Kaliṅgat-taraiyaṉ in the palace Periyamāḷigai at Rājēndraśōḻa-puram in Rājaśiṅgankuḷakkīḷ, a subdivision of Madurōdaya vaḷanāḍu, made a tax-free gift of lands to the temple of Tirumayilāḍupāṟai-uḍaiya-Mahādēva at Parākramapāṇḍya-chaturvedimaṅgalam in Nāṭṭāṟṟup-pōkku. The record was signed by Kāliṅgarāyan and Aḻagiyapāṇḍya-Muvēndavēḷāṉ of Śemmali-nāḍu.

4th year

ARIE/1928-1929/Stone inscriptions copied in 1928-29/1928-29/12 (page 7)
Placement
On a slab lying in a field in the Paṟaichchēri in the same village.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Māṟañjaḍaiyaṉ
Date
35+6th year
Language
Vaṭṭeḻuttu
Remarks
Records that Vēḷāṉ-Śāttaṉ of Irampāḍu in Karaikkāṉa-nāḍu erected two water-sheds, at Perumbaḻañji, one called Irāśakkar-taṇṇīrpperumbandal in the name of Irāśakkar of Tirukkōṭṭāṟu, and the other called Munnūṟṟuvapperum-bandal, and provided for burning lamps in them as well as for the maintenance of the men supplying water.
ARIE/1928-1929/Stone inscriptions copied in 1928-29/1928-29/13 (page 7)
Placement
Senbagaramanallur.--On the south wall of the maṇḍapa in front of the central shrine in the Jagannātha-Perumāḷ temple in the village.
Dynasty
Travancore
King
Vīra-Mārttāṇḍaṉ Śiṟaivāy-Mūttavar
Date
[Kollam] 703, Puraṭṭādi 11.
Language
Tamil
Remarks
Refers to the appointment of Āriyaṉ-Ulaguḍaipperumāḷ-Rāmachandradēvaṉ as the treasury accountant of the temple of Jagannātha-Perumāḷ at Śeṇbagarāmanallūr, a village to the east of Śrīvaramaṅgai in Vāṉa-nāḍu.
ARIE/1928-1929/Stone inscriptions copied in 1928-29/1928-29/14 (page 7)
Placement
On the wall of the maṇḍapa at the second entrance into the same temple.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Śaṅkaranārāyaṇa Veṉṟumaṇkoṇḍa Bhūtalavīra Rāmavarman.
Date
Kollam 720, Makara 4, ba. 2, Friday.
Language
Tamil
Remarks
Registers a gift of land by the king to the temple of Śeṇbagarāmaviṇṇagar-Emberumāṉ at Śeṇbagarāmanallūr, for the service of Śeṇbagarāmaṉ-śandi instituted in his name, and for the conduct of a special worship on the day of Aśvatī in the month of Āvaṇi, which was the day of his birth.

RAMNAD DISTRICT


TIRUPPATTUR TALUK


ARIE/1928-1929/Stone inscriptions copied in 1928-29/1928-29/16 (page 7)
Placement
Sivapuri.--On the north wall of the second prākāra in the Svayaṁprakāśēśvara temple in the village.
Dynasty
Chōḷa
King
Tribhuvanachakravartin Kulōttuṅga-Chōḷadēva.
Date
32nd year
Language

ARIE/1928-1929/Stone inscriptions copied in 1928-29/1928-29/492 (page 46)
Placement
On a third slab set up in the same prākāra.
Dynasty
Hoysaḷa
King
Pratāpachakravartin Vīra-Ballāḷadēva-rasa.
Date
Śaka 1255, Āṅgiras, Phālguṇa, ba. 10, Mīna, 16, Thurs-day.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Records gift of taxes on lands at Niruvāra, by the 14 (members of the assembly) of the village to the temple of Durgā-Bhagavatī. The gift was made with the permis-sion of Vayijappa-Daṇṇāyaka and other officers and in the presence of the chief queen Chikkāyi-Tāyigaḷu.

ARIE/1928-1929/Stone inscriptions copied in 1928-29/1928-29/494 (page 46)
Placement
On a fifth slab set up in the same prākāra.
Dynasty
Vijaya-nagara.
King
Kṛishṇarāya-Mahārāya
Date
Śaka 1450 (expir-ed), Sarvadhāri, Jyēshṭha, śu. 10.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Mentions Vijayaṇṇa-Voḍeya as governing Bārakūru-rājya under the seal of Timmaṇṇa-Voḍeya, who is stated to have been appointed by the king's vassal Kṛishṇarāya-Nāyaka. Records an assignment of 7(1/2) kāṭi (gold coin) out of the siddhāya-tax due from the village of Niruvāra, by Vijayaṇṇa, for the conduct of a special worship during the Navarātri days in the temple of Durgādēvī.

ARIE/1928-1929/Stone inscriptions copied in 1928-29/1928-29/503 (page 47)
Placement
On another slab set up in the same prākāra.
Dynasty
Vijayana-gara.
King
Kṛishṇarāya-Mahārāya
Date
Śaka 1440 (expired), Pramāthin, Jyēshṭha, śu. 15, Saturday.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Refers to Vijayappa-Oḍeya as governing Bārakūru under orders of his father Ratnappa-Oḍeya to whom it was entrusted by the king. Records an assignment by the chief, for the welfare and prosperity of the king, of 120 varāha of gold out of the taxes due from Peraḍūru, for offerings and perpetual lamps to god Anantadēva, and 60 varāha to a certain Sūrappa for doing these services. Peraḍūru is stated to be situated in Bandampaḷḷi-nāḍu, a sub-division of Bārakūru-rājya.

ARIE/1928-1929/List of stone inscriptions in the Bombay-Karnatak copied during the year 1928-29/1928-29/33 (page 43)

Bhuvanaikamalladēva
Date
Śaka 996, Ānanda, Pushya, śu. pañchamī, Sunday, Uttarā-yaṇa-saṁkrānti.
Language
Kannaḍa (prose & verse)
Remarks

Kannaḍa (prose & verse)

Registers the gift of land and money for the feeding of Jaina ascetics and for the worship, etc., of Pārśvanātha set up by Nāgasiriyauvve, the lay disciple of Sakaḷachandra-Bhaṭṭāraka of the Kāṇūra-gaṇa and the Mūla-saṅgha. The gift was made when the Five Hundred Svāmis of Ayyā-voḷe together with the prabhus, muṁmuridaṇḍas, and the thousand nānādēśis of Halasige Twelve-Thousand and Banavase Twelve-Thousand were assembled as a Mahā-nāḍu at Kandagāle, the maḷigeyamane of the Kaṁnaḍa-Four-thousand district.

ARIE/1928-1929/List of stone inscriptions in the Bombay-Karnatak copied during the year 1928-29/1928-29/91 (page 47)
Placement
Mantur.--On a stone set up in front of the temple of Rāma-liṅga.
Dynasty
Western Chāḷukya
King
Jagadēkamalladēva
Date
Śaka 962, Vikrama, Mārgaśira, śu. 5, Sunday.
Language
Kannaḍa (prose & verse)
Remarks
Damaged at the end. Records the gift of money made, to Madhusūdanayya and other Mahājanas of Maṁṭūru, for the excavation of a tank called Raṭṭasamudra, by the Mahāsāmanta Eṟeyamma, who was born of the ‘Raṭṭa-vaṁśa’ and was ‘the lord of Lattalūr-puravara.’ The king is stated to have been then ruling from the ‘nelevīḍu’ at Heṭṭaḷakeṟe.

Sinda
King
Chāvuṇḍadēva
Date
Śaka 1076, Yuva, Pushya, śu 14, Monday, Utta-rāyaṇa-saṁkrānti.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Registers a grant of land made by Mahāmātya Sōmanātha-Nāyaka, Gayādhara-Nāyaka, and others, with the permission of the queen Lakshmādēvī who was governing Posavūr, to the temple of Mallikārjuna at Kapilāśrama in Posavūr. It also states that the āchārya of the temple was Kēdāra, disciple of Jñānaśakti.

ARIE/1928-1929/List of stone inscriptions in the Bombay-Karnatak copied during the year 1928-29/1928-29/151 (page 50)

King

Date

Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Damaged. Registers the grant of the village Suggivāḍa situated in Haṅgarage-12 as Paramēśvara-datti to the 500 Mahājanas of the Mahāgrahāra Kaḍakeṟe, made by Mahādēva-Daṇḍanāyaka, with the permission of the Daṇḍanāyaka Tikkarasa, who was the adhikāri of the Bāgaḍage-nāḍu and who is here called the gandhavāraṇa of the Pradhäna Sōvaṇa-Daṇḍanātha, while Mahā-maṇḍalēśvara Vīra-Bijjaḷadēvarasa and Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Vīrā-Vikramādityadēvarasa of the Sinda family were governing Kisukāḍu-70, Bāgaḍage-70, Nareyaṁgal-12 Keḷavāḍi-300 and Kariviḍi-30. The gift was made for the merit of Chāvuṇḍarasa of the Sinda family on the occasion of Tikkarasa's visit to Kaḍakeṟe.

ARIE/1928-1929/List of stone inscriptions in the Bombay-Karnatak copied during the year 1928-29/1928-29/193 (page 53)

Language
Kannaḍa

The gift was made at the instance of the king and was to be protected by the ruling kings, trivargas, samayas and the One-Thousand.

Tribhuvanamalla [Vīra Sō]mēśvaradēvā
Date
5th year, Parā-bhava, .... Vyatīpāta; 6th year, Plavaṅga.
Language
Kannaḍa & Sanskṛit
Remarks
Badly damaged. Records a gift of land made to the Brāhmaṇas of the five brahmapuris of Aṇṇigeṟe by Kēśavabhaṭṭayya-Daṇḍanāyaka who was a Perggaḍe of Beḷvala-nāḍu under Mahāpradhāna Ballaya-Sāhaṇi, a subordinate of Bammidēva-Daṇḍādhipa. Also records another gift of land to Brāhmaṇas made on the second date by Haḍavaḷa Basavayya, the head of the town (i.e., Aṇṇigeṟe).

ARIE/1928-1929/List of stone inscriptions in the Bombay-Karnatak copied during the year 1928-29/1928-29/233 (page 55)
Placement
On a third slab in the same place.

Western Chāḷukya
King
Pratāpachakravarti Jagadēkamalla
Date
5th year, Dundubhi, Phālguṇa, ... eclipse.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Damaged. Śaka 981, Vikāri, Mārgaśira, śu. 2, Wednesday, Pūrvāshāḍha, Kaulava-karaṇa, Gaṇḍa-Tōga.
Language
Sanskṛit & Kannaḍa
Remarks
Records the death, by saṁnyasana-vidhi in the Ghaṭānta-kiya-basadi at Moraṁba, of the Jaina teacher Nāga-chandra-Siddhāntadēva, a disciple of Jayakīrttidēva of the Yāpanīya-saṁgha. Nāgachandra-yati is praised as a great scholar and is given the biruda of Mantrachūḍā-maṇi. The nisidhi stone (on which the inscription is incised) was set up by his disciple Kanakaśakti-Siddhān-tadēva.
ARIE/1928-1929/List of stone inscriptions in the Bombay-Karnatak copied during the year 1928-29/1928-29/240 (page 56)

ARIE/1928-1929/List of stone inscriptions in the Bombay-Karnatak copied during the year 1928-29/1928-29/241 (page 56)
Placement
Navalli,--On a slab set up in front of the temple of Kalamēś-vara.
Dynasty
Western Chāḷukya
King
Tribhuvanamalladēva
Date
Chāḷukya-Vikrama year 46, Plava-Chaitra, puṇ-ṇami, Monday, lunar eclipse.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Registers a gift made for worship, offerings, etc., to the god Svayambhu-Kalidēva at the agrahārā Nāppoḷe and for the maintenance of a Bālasikshe by Daṇḍanāyaka Sāyipayya and others, at the request of Ballarasa, when Mahāpradhāna Maneverggaḍe Kēśava-Chamūpa was governing the Beḷvola-300 and the Puligeṟe-300.

ARIE/1928-1929/List of stone inscriptions in the Bombay-Karnatak copied during the year 1928-29/1928-29/246 (page 57)
Placement
On a slab set up in the temple
Dynasty
Rāshṭrakūṭa
King
Amōghavarshadēva
Date
Śaka 793 Khara, Phālguṇa, śu. 1, Wednesday, Hastā.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Records that Dēvaṇayya, who was the governor of the Beḷvola-300 exempted the Brahmans of Sisuḷahāḻu from taxes on ghee, with the approval of the fifty Mahājanas of the village, on the occasion of a lunar eclipse.
